2024-07-11 07:52:19====>获取就诊信息:Select Decode(B.急诊,1,'2','1') As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,'' As wardCode,'' As wardName,'' As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人挂号记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D
                             Where A.Id=B.记录id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id
                               And A.id='BC99C73D-50F4-4E85-90C5-853240095F46'
                            Union All
                            Select '3' As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,E.编码 As wardCode,E.简称 As wardName,B.床号 As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人入院记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D,部门 E
                             Where A.Id=B.事件id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id And B.病房id=E.资源id(+)
                               And A.id='BC99C73D-50F4-4E85-90C5-853240095F46'

2024-07-11 08:37:57====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '99047733-b757-44fd-a877-fcdfd0031745'
                            And a.事件id = 'C4807ACC-AE86-4999-ADA8-E95ACCE795AC'
                            And a.组序号 in (12)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 08:37:57====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '99047733-b757-44fd-a877-fcdfd0031745'
                            And a.事件id = 'C4807ACC-AE86-4999-ADA8-E95ACCE795AC'
                            And a.组序号 in (13)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 09:56:38====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'D78AD656-6CAA-281E-E054-9CDC71ADEB60'
                            And a.事件id = '1C623366-A025-3302-E064-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.组序号 in (46)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 10:12:57====>获取就诊信息:Select Decode(B.急诊,1,'2','1') As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,'' As wardCode,'' As wardName,'' As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人挂号记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D
                             Where A.Id=B.记录id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id
                               And A.id='EC8B0E54-BD2E-45AF-A429-B9E6BEC2A6CB'
                            Union All
                            Select '3' As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,E.编码 As wardCode,E.简称 As wardName,B.床号 As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人入院记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D,部门 E
                             Where A.Id=B.事件id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id And B.病房id=E.资源id(+)
                               And A.id='EC8B0E54-BD2E-45AF-A429-B9E6BEC2A6CB'

2024-07-11 10:12:59====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '0DE081B8-E3E1-4F3A-8B52-1FF36BB2EF11'
                            And a.事件id = 'EC8B0E54-BD2E-45AF-A429-B9E6BEC2A6CB'
                            And a.组序号 in (14)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 10:50:53====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '99047733-b757-44fd-a877-fcdfd0031745'
                            And a.事件id = 'C4807ACC-AE86-4999-ADA8-E95ACCE795AC'
                            And a.组序号 in (29)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 10:58:39====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D5-7B60-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = 'F00F5F90-4651-4BDB-BC2A-A0F11EEF726A'
                            And a.组序号 in (11)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 10:58:39====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D5-7B60-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = 'F00F5F90-4651-4BDB-BC2A-A0F11EEF726A'
                            And a.组序号 in (12)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 11:42:45====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'fbf12dd2-8af7-4555-8b4a-85bb9c5e38b7'
                            And a.事件id = '9B298C79-1650-430C-8CA0-11F9F9714EC6'
                            And a.组序号 in (13)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 11:42:45====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'fbf12dd2-8af7-4555-8b4a-85bb9c5e38b7'
                            And a.事件id = '9B298C79-1650-430C-8CA0-11F9F9714EC6'
                            And a.组序号 in (14)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 11:45:27====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'fbf12dd2-8af7-4555-8b4a-85bb9c5e38b7'
                            And a.事件id = '9B298C79-1650-430C-8CA0-11F9F9714EC6'
                            And a.组序号 in (14)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 11:46:11====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'fbf12dd2-8af7-4555-8b4a-85bb9c5e38b7'
                            And a.事件id = '9B298C79-1650-430C-8CA0-11F9F9714EC6'
                            And a.组序号 in (13)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 11:57:56====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '698D5BCE-AD7D-4C9B-B7A3-1D84005C4C5A'
                            And a.事件id = 'BAB3ED54-CE16-4676-818C-7B669E0BE48B'
                            And a.组序号 in (12)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 11:57:57====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '698D5BCE-AD7D-4C9B-B7A3-1D84005C4C5A'
                            And a.事件id = 'BAB3ED54-CE16-4676-818C-7B669E0BE48B'
                            And a.组序号 in (14)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 11:59:59====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '698D5BCE-AD7D-4C9B-B7A3-1D84005C4C5A'
                            And a.事件id = 'BAB3ED54-CE16-4676-818C-7B669E0BE48B'
                            And a.组序号 in (15)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人挂号记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D

2024-07-11 16:21:05====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'b4e16ee5-af4c-4353-98bf-48e571fe68b9'
                            And a.事件id = '83A389A0-98DA-43AB-87FE-448585765C43'
                            And a.组序号 in (15)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-07-11 16:21:05====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'b4e16ee5-af4c-4353-98bf-48e571fe68b9'
                            And a.事件id = '83A389A0-98DA-43AB-87FE-448585765C43'
                            And a.组序号 in (16)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno
